GT: -c0*beta*v - beta*exp(-Abs(x))*v - mu*(c1 - x**c2)*v - omega0**c3*x**c4
Candidate formulas: 56

GT (fixed) simplifies to a polynomial-in-\(x\) times \(v\), plus an \(\exp(-|x|)\) damping term, plus a pure \(x^3\) restoring term:
\[
\text{GT}= -1.1598282332023\,x^3 \;+\; v\Big(0.752289977167006\,x^2 - 1.366305954203476\Big)\;-\;0.307007988518235\,v\,e^{-|x|}.
\]
Key structural requirements for any exact global match (for all real \(x,v,t\)):
1) Must contain the non-analytic term \(v\,e^{-|x|}\) with the absolute value in the exponent (cannot be replaced by \(e^{kx}\), \(\log\), rational, etc. globally).
2) No dependence on \(t\).
3) No extra nonlinearities in \(v\) (only linear in \(v\)).
4) Polynomial terms must match exactly: \(x^3\) term and \(v\), \(v x^2\) terms with correct coefficients; no extra \(x\), constants, etc.

Now check candidates:

1. Has \(v\exp(c4 x)\) (no \(|x|\)) and an extra cosine-of-log term. Can’t produce \(v e^{-|x|}\) globally; cosine term can be zeroed (set \(c5=0\)) but still lacks \(e^{-|x|}\). **No**.

4. Has \(v\log(c4|c5 x|+1)\) and \(v\exp(c7 x)\). Log can’t equal \(e^{-|x|}\) globally; also exp lacks \(|x|\). **No**.
